<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dilemma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δίλημμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dílēmma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">double proposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δι-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">di-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λῆμμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lêmma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">premise, proposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***динамо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:динамо.html>дина́мо</a> (12866)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динамо.html>дина́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dinámo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>dynamo</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динамо.html>дина́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dinámo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a girl or a woman who flirts without offering (promised) sex; cocktease</li></ol>

***динозавр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:динозавр.html>диноза́вр</a> (15177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Dinosauria</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δεινός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deinós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scary, awful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σαῦρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">saûros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lizard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динозавр.html>диноза́вр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dinozávr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динозавр.html>диноза́вра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динозавр.html>диноза́вры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:динозавр.html>диноза́вров</a></b>)

***дипломат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́т</a> (4696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">diplomate</i>. The sense “briefcase” arose from the custom of diplomats to carry briefcases.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diplomát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>diplomat (person who is accredited to represent a government)</li>
<li>briefcase</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">диплома́нт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diplománt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> that includes an extra letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">n</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломный.html>дипло́мный</a> (19173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диплом.html>дипло́м</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diplóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломный.html>дипло́мный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diplómnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diploma, certificate of degree
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломный.html>дипло́мная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>diplómnaja</b> rabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">degree work/research/thesis</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломный.html>дипло́мный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>diplómnyj</b> proékt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">graduation thesis/work</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диплом.html>дипло́м</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">diplóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дипломированный.html>дипломи́рованный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">diplomírovannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́са</a> (23625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">directrice</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́са</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">direktrísa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́сы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́с</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директор.html>дире́ктор</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>female director</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> headmistress</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́са</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">direktrísa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́сы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:директриса.html>директри́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> directrix</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дирижер.html>дирижёр</a> (10276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably an Inner-Russian formation as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижировать.html>дирижи́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dirižírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dīrigere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to direct, steer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижер.html>дирижёр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dirižór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижер.html>дирижёра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижер.html>дирижёры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижер.html>дирижёров</a></b>)

***дирижировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дирижировать.html>дирижи́ровать</a> (21211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">dirigieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижировать.html>дирижи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dirižírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(orchestra, choir)</i> to conduct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tp orchestrate</li></ol>

***диск.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a> (3732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δίσκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dískos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a circular plate suited for hurling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δικείν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dikeín</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurl, to launch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">disk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>ди́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>ди́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>ди́сков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disk, disc</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> discus, platter</li>
<li>cartridge-drum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> CD, compact disc</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***дискредитировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дискредитировать.html>дискредити́ровать</a> (22569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">diskreditieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дискредитировать.html>дискредити́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">diskreditírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to discredit, to compromise, to disgrace</li></ol>
